\DoxyCodeLine{1585                                                                \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1586   \textcolor{comment}{// We had a bug which produced invalid version 13 data (see}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1587   \textcolor{comment}{// crbug.com/1284506). This compatibility mode tries to first read the data}}
